import tailwindcss from '@tailwindcss/vite';
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react';
import path from 'path';
import {defineConfig, loadEnv} from 'vite';

export default defineConfig(({mode}) => {
  const env = loadEnv(mode, '.', '');
  return {
    base: './',
    plugins: [react(), tailwindcss()],
    define: {
      'process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY': JSON.stringify(env.GEMINI_API_KEY),
    },
    resolve: {
      alias: {
        '@': path.resolve(__dirname, '.'),
      },
    },
    server: {
      // HMR is disabled in AI Studio via DISABLE_HMR env var.
      // Do not modifyÃ¢Â€Â”file watching is disabled to prevent flickering during agent edits.
      hmr: process.env.DISABLE_HMR !== 'true',
      proxy: {
        '/api': {
          target: env.ASSISTANT_API_ORIGIN || 'http://localhost:3001',
          changeOrigin: true,
        },
      },
    },
  };
});

import 'dotenv/config';
import express from 'express';
import fs from 'node:fs';
import path from 'node:path';
import { fileURLToPath } from 'node:url';

const __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
const __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);
const projectRoot = path.resolve(__dirname, '..');
const distDir = path.join(projectRoot, 'dist');

const app = express();
const port = Number(process.env.PORT || 3001);

app.use(express.json({ limit: '1mb' }));

function isMessage(value) {
  if (!value || typeof value !== 'object') {
    return false;
  }

  return (
    (value.role === 'user' || value.role === 'assistant' || value.role === 'system')
    && typeof value.content === 'string'
    && value.content.trim().length > 0
  );
}

function buildSystemPrompt(context) {
  const contextLines = [
    context.activeTab ? `PestaÃ±a activa: ${context.activeTab}.` : null,
    context.selectedDateLabel ? `Fecha seleccionada: ${context.selectedDateLabel}.` : null,
    context.selectedDate ? `Fecha ISO seleccionada: ${context.selectedDate}.` : null,
  ].filter(Boolean);

  return [
    'Eres el asistente IA de Falles360.',
    'Responde en espaÃ±ol de forma breve, Ãºtil y accionable.',
    'Da recomendaciones pensadas para Fallas en Valencia.',
    'Si propones un plan, ordÃ©nalo en una secuencia clara y prÃ¡ctica.',
    contextLines.length > 0 ? `Contexto actual de la interfaz: ${contextLines.join(' ')}` : null,
  ].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
}

function isMapPoint(value) {
  return (
    Array.isArray(value)
    && value.length === 2
    && value.every((coordinate) => typeof coordinate === 'number' && Number.isFinite(coordinate))
  );
}

function formatStreetName(step) {
  if (typeof step?.name === 'string' && step.name.trim().length > 0) {
    return step.name.trim();
  }

  if (typeof step?.ref === 'string' && step.ref.trim().length > 0) {
    return step.ref.trim();
  }

  return 'la via indicada';
}

function buildRouteInstruction(step) {
  const streetName = formatStreetName(step);
  const maneuver = step?.maneuver ?? {};
  const modifier = typeof maneuver.modifier === 'string' ? maneuver.modifier : '';
  const type = typeof maneuver.type === 'string' ? maneuver.type : '';

  if (type === 'depart') {
    return `Sal de tu posicion y avanza por ${streetName}.`;
  }

  if (type === 'arrive') {
    return 'Has llegado a tu destino.';
  }

  if (type === 'roundabout' || type === 'rotary') {
    return `En la rotonda, sigue las indicaciones hacia ${streetName}.`;
  }

  if (type === 'continue' || type === 'new name') {
    return `Continua por ${streetName}.`;
  }

  if (type === 'fork') {
    if (modifier === 'left') {
      return `Mantente a la izquierda hacia ${streetName}.`;
    }

    if (modifier === 'right') {
      return `Mantente a la derecha hacia ${streetName}.`;
    }

    return `Sigue el desvio hacia ${streetName}.`;
  }

  if (type === 'merge') {
    return `Incorporate hacia ${streetName}.`;
  }

  if (type === 'end of road') {
    if (modifier === 'left') {
      return `Al final de la via, gira a la izquierda hacia ${streetName}.`;
    }

    if (modifier === 'right') {
      return `Al final de la via, gira a la derecha hacia ${streetName}.`;
    }
  }

  if (type === 'turn') {
    if (modifier === 'left' || modifier === 'slight left' || modifier === 'sharp left') {
      return `Gira a la izquierda hacia ${streetName}.`;
    }

    if (modifier === 'right' || modifier === 'slight right' || modifier === 'sharp right') {
      return `Gira a la derecha hacia ${streetName}.`;
    }

    if (modifier === 'uturn') {
      return `Haz un cambio de sentido hacia ${streetName}.`;
    }

    return `Gira hacia ${streetName}.`;
  }

  return `Sigue hacia ${streetName}.`;
}

app.post('/api/assistant', async (request, response) => {
  const apiKey = process.env.OPENROUTER_API_KEY;
  const model = process.env.OPENROUTER_MODEL || 'openrouter/free';
  const messages = Array.isArray(request.body?.messages) ? request.body.messages.filter(isMessage) : [];
  const context = request.body?.context ?? {};

  if (!apiKey) {
    response.status(500).json({
      message: 'Falta OPENROUTER_API_KEY en el entorno del servidor.',
    });
    return;
  }

  if (messages.length === 0) {
    response.status(400).json({
      message: 'Debes enviar al menos un mensaje.',
    });
    return;
  }

  try {
    const upstream = await fetch('https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/chat/completions', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        Authorization: `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'HTTP-Referer': process.env.APP_URL || 'http://localhost:3000',
        'X-Title': 'Falles360 Dashboard Assistant',
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model,
        messages: [
          { role: 'system', content: buildSystemPrompt(context) },
          ...messages,
        ],
      }),
    });

    const payload = await upstream.json().catch(() => null);

    if (!upstream.ok) {
      response.status(upstream.status).json({
        message: payload?.error?.message || payload?.message || 'No se pudo completar la solicitud a OpenRouter.',
      });
      return;
    }

    const content = payload?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content;

    if (typeof content !== 'string' || content.trim() === '') {
      response.status(502).json({
        message: 'OpenRouter no devolviÃ³ contenido utilizable.',
      });
      return;
    }

    response.json({
      content,
      model: payload?.model || model,
    });
  } catch (error) {
    response.status(500).json({
      message: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Error inesperado al consultar OpenRouter.',
    });
  }
});

app.post('/api/route', async (request, response) => {
  const origin = request.body?.origin;
  const destination = request.body?.destination;
  const profile = request.body?.profile === 'driving' ? 'driving' : 'walking';

  if (!isMapPoint(origin) || !isMapPoint(destination)) {
    response.status(400).json({
      message: 'Debes enviar origen y destino validos.',
    });
    return;
  }

  const [originLat, originLng] = origin;
  const [destinationLat, destinationLng] = destination;

  const upstreamUrl = new URL(
    `https://router.project-osrm.org/route/v1/${profile}/${originLng},${originLat};${destinationLng},${destinationLat}`
  );
  upstreamUrl.searchParams.set('overview', 'full');
  upstreamUrl.searchParams.set('geometries', 'geojson');
  upstreamUrl.searchParams.set('steps', 'true');

  try {
    const upstream = await fetch(upstreamUrl);
    const payload = await upstream.json().catch(() => null);

    if (!upstream.ok || payload?.code !== 'Ok') {
      response.status(502).json({
        message: payload?.message || 'No se pudo obtener una ruta valida.',
      });
      return;
    }

    const bestRoute = payload?.routes?.[0];

    if (!bestRoute?.geometry?.coordinates || !Array.isArray(bestRoute.geometry.coordinates)) {
      response.status(502).json({
        message: 'El motor de rutas no devolvio geometria utilizable.',
      });
      return;
    }

    const steps = Array.isArray(bestRoute.legs)
      ? bestRoute.legs.flatMap((leg) =>
          Array.isArray(leg?.steps)
            ? leg.steps.map((step) => ({
                instruction: buildRouteInstruction(step),
                distanceMeters: Number(step.distance) || 0,
                durationSeconds: Number(step.duration) || 0,
                streetName: formatStreetName(step),
              }))
            : []
        )
      : [];

    response.json({
      geometry: bestRoute.geometry.coordinates.map(([lng, lat]) => [lat, lng]),
      distanceMeters: Number(bestRoute.distance) || 0,
      durationSeconds: Number(bestRoute.duration) || 0,
      steps,
    });
  } catch (error) {
    response.status(500).json({
      message: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Error inesperado al calcular la ruta.',
    });
  }
});

if (fs.existsSync(distDir)) {
  app.use(express.static(distDir));

  app.get('*', (request, response, next) => {
    if (request.path.startsWith('/api/')) {
      next();
      return;
    }

    response.sendFile(path.join(distDir, 'index.html'));
  });
}

app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(`Assistant server listening on http://localhost:${port}`);
});

interface ProfileApiResponse {
  ok?: boolean;
  profile?: {
    type?: string;
    name?: string;
    email?: string | null;
  };
}

interface StoredViewerPreferences {
  name?: string;
  location?: string;
  avatar?: string;
}

const VIEWER_PREFERENCES_KEY = 'falles360.viewer-preferences.v1';

function resolveProfileEndpoint(): string {
  if (typeof window === 'undefined') {
    return '/api/profile.php';
  }

  const pathname = window.location.pathname;
  const dashboardIndex = pathname.indexOf('/dashboard');

  if (dashboardIndex === -1) {
    return '/api/profile.php';
  }

  const basePath = pathname.slice(0, dashboardIndex);
  return `${basePath || ''}/api/profile.php`;
}

function buildViewerHandle(name: string): string {
  const normalized = name
    .toLowerCase()
    .normalize('NFD')
    .replace(/[\u0300-\u036f]/g, '')
    .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '');

  return `@${normalized || 'falles360'}`;
}

function buildViewerAvatar(name: string, accessType: AppViewer['accessType']): string {
  return `https://i.pravatar.cc/150?u=${encodeURIComponent(`${accessType}-${name.trim() || 'falles360'}`)}`;
}

function readStoredViewerPreferences(): StoredViewerPreferences | null {
  if (typeof window === 'undefined') {
    return null;
  }

  try {
    const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(VIEWER_PREFERENCES_KEY);
    if (!raw) {
      return null;
    }

    const parsed = JSON.parse(raw) as StoredViewerPreferences;
    return {
      name: typeof parsed.name === 'string' ? parsed.name : undefined,
      location: typeof parsed.location === 'string' ? parsed.location : undefined,
      avatar: typeof parsed.avatar === 'string' ? parsed.avatar : undefined,
    };
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

function writeStoredViewerPreferences(viewer: AppViewer): void {
  if (typeof window === 'undefined') {
    return;
  }

  window.localStorage.setItem(
    VIEWER_PREFERENCES_KEY,
    JSON.stringify({
      name: viewer.name,
      location: viewer.location,
      avatar: viewer.avatar,
    })
  );
}

function applyStoredViewerPreferences(baseViewer: AppViewer, preferences: StoredViewerPreferences | null): AppViewer {
  if (!preferences) {
    return baseViewer;
  }

  const resolvedName = preferences.name?.trim() || baseViewer.name;

  return {
    ...baseViewer,
    name: resolvedName,
    location: preferences.location?.trim() || baseViewer.location,
    avatar: preferences.avatar?.trim() || baseViewer.avatar,
    handle: buildViewerHandle(resolvedName),
  };
}

function mapProfileToViewer(profile: NonNullable<ProfileApiResponse['profile']>): AppViewer {
  const accessType = profile.type === 'guest' ? 'guest' : 'user';
  const baseViewer = accessType === 'guest' ? APP_GUEST_VIEWER : APP_VIEWER;
  const resolvedName = (profile.name || '').trim() || baseViewer.name;

  return {
    ...baseViewer,
    name: resolvedName,
    handle: buildViewerHandle(resolvedName),
    avatar: buildViewerAvatar(resolvedName, accessType),
    accessType,
    isRegistered: accessType === 'user',
  };
}

type DashboardIcon = React.ComponentType<{ className?: string }>;

function DashboardSurface({
  isDarkMode,
  className,
  children,
}: {
  isDarkMode: boolean;
  className?: string;
  children: ReactNode;
}) {
  return (
    <div
      className={cn(
        'rounded-[2.35rem] border p-6 transition-all duration-300',
        isDarkMode ? 'border-white/10 bg-white/5' : 'border-gray-100 bg-white shadow-xl',
        className
      )}
    >
      {children}
    </div>
  );
}

function DashboardMetric({
  isDarkMode,
  icon: Icon,
  label,
  value,
  helper,
}: {
  isDarkMode: boolean;
  icon: DashboardIcon;
  label: string;
  value: string;
  helper: string;
}) {
  return (
    <div
      className={cn(
        'rounded-[1.7rem] border p-4',
        isDarkMode ? 'border-white/10 bg-white/[0.045]' : 'border-slate-100 bg-slate-50/70'
      )}
    >
      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
        <div
          className={cn(
            'flex h-11 w-11 items-center justify-center rounded-[1rem]',
            isDarkMode ? 'bg-brand/14 text-brand' : 'bg-brand/10 text-brand'
          )}
        >
          <Icon className="h-5 w-5" />
        </div>
        <div className="min-w-0">
          <p className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em] opacity-45">{label}</p>
          <p className="mt-1 text-[1.45rem] font-black leading-none tracking-tight">{value}</p>
        </div>
      </div>
      <p className="mt-3 text-sm font-bold leading-5 opacity-60">{helper}</p>
    </div>
  );
}

function SectionHero({
  isDarkMode,
  eyebrow,
  title,
  description,
  children,
  actions,
  className,
}: {
  isDarkMode: boolean;
  eyebrow: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  children?: ReactNode;
  actions?: ReactNode;
  className?: string;
}) {
  return (
    <DashboardSurface
      isDarkMode={isDarkMode}
      className={cn(
        'relative overflow-hidden border-transparent bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_right,rgba(255,99,33,0.12),transparent_26%),linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.96),rgba(255,247,241,0.96))]',
        isDarkMode && 'bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_right,rgba(255,99,33,0.18),transparent_26%),linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.06),rgba(255,255,255,0.04))]',
        className
      )}
    >
      <div className="pointer-events-none absolute -right-10 -top-10 h-36 w-36 rounded-full bg-brand/10 blur-3xl" />
      <div className="relative z-10 flex flex-col gap-6 xl:flex-row xl:items-end xl:justify-between">
        <div className="max-w-2xl">
          <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full bg-brand/10 px-3 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-brand">
            <Sparkles className="h-3.5 w-3.5" />
            {eyebrow}
          </div>
          <h2 className="mt-4 text-[2.2rem] font-black leading-[0.95] tracking-[-0.05em] sm:text-[2.7rem]">
            {title}
          </h2>
          <p className="mt-3 max-w-2xl text-[15px] font-bold leading-6 opacity-65">{description}</p>
        </div>
        {actions ? <div className="relative z-10 flex flex-wrap gap-3">{actions}</div> : null}
      </div>
      {children ? <div className="relative z-10 mt-6">{children}</div> : null}
    </DashboardSurface>
  );
}

export default function App() {
  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState('');
  const [selectedCategory, setSelectedCategory] = useState<'Todas' | 'Principal' | 'Infantil' | 'Experimental'>('Todas');
  const [selectedFalla, setSelectedFalla] = useState<Falla | null>(null);
  const [favorites, setFavorites] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('Mapa');
  const [selectedDate, setSelectedDate] = useState(() => toIsoDate(new Date()));
  const [isDarkMode, setIsDarkMode] = useState(false);
  const [showDetail, setShowDetail] = useState<Falla | null>(null);
  const [navigationFalla, setNavigationFalla] = useState<Falla | null>(null);
  const [activeRouteFallaId, setActiveRouteFallaId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [mapStyleId, setMapStyleId] = useState<MapStyleId>('city');
  const [viewer, setViewer] = useState<AppViewer>(APP_VIEWER);
  const [isProfileSettingsOpen, setIsProfileSettingsOpen] = useState(false);
  const { userPosition, locationStatus, requestLocation } = useUserLocation();

  useEffect(() => {
    const storedPreferences = readStoredViewerPreferences();
    if (storedPreferences) {
      setViewer((current) => applyStoredViewerPreferences(current, storedPreferences));
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (import.meta.env.DEV) {
      return;
    }

    const controller = new AbortController();

    fetch(resolveProfileEndpoint(), {
      credentials: 'same-origin',
      signal: controller.signal,
    })
      .then(async (response) => {
        if (!response.ok) {
          throw new Error('profile_unavailable');
        }

        return response.json() as Promise<ProfileApiResponse>;
      })
      .then((payload) => {
        if (payload.ok && payload.profile) {
          setViewer(applyStoredViewerPreferences(mapProfileToViewer(payload.profile), readStoredViewerPreferences()));
        }
      })
      .catch(() => {
        // Mantiene el viewer local cuando el endpoint no esta disponible.
      });

    return () => {
      controller.abort();
    };
  }, []);

  const filteredFallas = useMemo(() => {
    return FALLAS_MOCK.filter((falla) => {
      const matchesSearch =
        falla.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase())
        || falla.neighborhood.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase());
      const matchesCategory = selectedCategory === 'Todas' || falla.category === selectedCategory;
      return matchesSearch && matchesCategory;
    });
  }, [searchQuery, selectedCategory]);

  const toggleFavorite = (id: string, e?: React.MouseEvent) => {
    if (e) {
      e.stopPropagation();
    }
    setFavorites((prev) => (prev.includes(id) ? prev.filter((f) => f !== id) : [...prev, id]));
  };

  const cridaEvent = useMemo(
    () => EVENTS_MOCK.find((event) => event.title.toLowerCase().includes('crid')) ?? null,
    []
  );

  const filteredEvents = useMemo(
    () => EVENTS_MOCK.filter((event) => event.date === selectedDate),
    [selectedDate]
  );

  const selectedDateLabel = useMemo(
    () => formatLongDate(fromIsoDate(selectedDate)),
    [selectedDate]
  );

  const activeRouteFalla = useMemo(
    () => FALLAS_MOCK.find((falla) => falla.id === activeRouteFallaId) ?? null,
    [activeRouteFallaId]
  );

  const selectedDateEvents = useMemo(
    () => [...filteredEvents].sort((left, right) => left.time.localeCompare(right.time)),
    [filteredEvents]
  );

  const favoriteFallas = useMemo(
    () => FALLAS_MOCK.filter((falla) => favorites.includes(falla.id)),
    [favorites]
  );

  const mostLikedPosts = useMemo(
    () => [...SOCIAL_POSTS].sort((left, right) => right.likes - left.likes).slice(0, 3),
    []
  );

  const principalFallasCount = useMemo(
    () => FALLAS_MOCK.filter((falla) => falla.category === 'Principal').length,
    []
  );

  const uniqueNeighborhoodsCount = useMemo(
    () => new Set(FALLAS_MOCK.map((falla) => falla.neighborhood)).size,
    []
  );

  const liveEventsCount = useMemo(
    () => EVENTS_MOCK.filter((event) => event.isLive).length,
    []
  );

  const nextSelectedDateEvent = selectedDateEvents[0] ?? null;
  const routeFocusFalla = navigationFalla ?? selectedFalla ?? activeRouteFalla;
  const isTvTab = activeTab === 'TV';
  const showTopRail = activeTab === 'Agenda' || activeTab === 'Fallas';
  const hasDockedNavigation = activeTab === 'Mapa' && Boolean(navigationFalla);

  const handleNavigateToFalla = (falla: Falla) => {
    setActiveTab('Mapa');
    setShowDetail(null);
    setSelectedFalla(falla);
    setNavigationFalla(falla);
    setActiveRouteFallaId(falla.id);
  };

  const handleSaveViewerSettings = (settings: Pick<AppViewer, 'name' | 'location' | 'avatar'>) => {
    setViewer((current) => {
      const nextViewer: AppViewer = {
        ...current,
        name: settings.name.trim() || current.name,
        location: settings.location.trim() || current.location,
        avatar: settings.avatar.trim() || current.avatar,
        handle: buildViewerHandle(settings.name.trim() || current.name),
      };

      writeStoredViewerPreferences(nextViewer);
      return nextViewer;
    });
    setIsProfileSettingsOpen(false);
  };

    switch (activeTab) {
      case 'Mapa':
        return (

              'grid grid-cols-1 items-start gap-8',

          >
            <div className="min-w-0 space-y-6">
              <div
                className={cn(
                  'grid grid-cols-1 gap-6',
                  hasDockedNavigation ? '2xl:grid-cols-[minmax(300px,0.84fr)_minmax(0,1fr)]' : 'xl:grid-cols-[minmax(320px,0.82fr)_minmax(0,1fr)]'

                <div className="min-w-0">
                  <CountdownCard isDarkMode={isDarkMode} event={cridaEvent} />

                  isDarkMode && 'bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_right,rgba(255,99,33,0.18),transparent_24%),linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.06),rgba(255,255,255,0.04))]'

                <div className="pointer-events-none absolute -right-10 top-0 h-32 w-32 rounded-full bg-brand/10 blur-3xl" />
                <div className="relative z-10 flex flex-col gap-5 lg:flex-row lg:items-start lg:justify-between">
                  <div className="max-w-3xl">
                    <p className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-brand">Mapa fallero</p>
                    <h2 className="mt-2 text-[1.9rem] font-black leading-[0.95] tracking-[-0.04em] sm:text-[2.35rem]">
                      Menos bloques, mÃ¡s mapa y una ruta mÃ¡s clara.
                    </h2>
                    <p className="mt-3 max-w-2xl text-sm font-bold leading-6 opacity-60">
                      El dashboard ahora arranca con lo Ãºtil: calendario, foco actual y accesos directos sin tarjetas de relleno.
                    </p>
                  </div>

                    <button
                      type="button"
                      onClick={() => setActiveTab('Social')}

                        'inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-[1.15rem] px-4 py-3 text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-all',
                        isDarkMode ? 'bg-white/10 text-white hover:bg-white/14' : 'bg-slate-950 text-white hover:bg-slate-800'
                      )}
                    >
                      <MessageCircle className="h-4 w-4" />
                      Ir al feed
                    </button>

                      type="button"

                        'inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-[1.15rem] px-4 py-3 text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-all',
                        isDarkMode ? 'bg-white/8 text-white/82 hover:bg-white/12' : 'bg-white text-slate-700 hover:bg-slate-50'
                      )}
                    >

                      Ver agenda
                    </button>
                    {routeFocusFalla && (
                      <button
                        type="button"
                        onClick={() => {
                          setNavigationFalla(routeFocusFalla);
                          setActiveRouteFallaId(routeFocusFalla.id);
                        }}
                        className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-[1.15rem] bg-brand px-4 py-3 text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-white shadow-xl shadow-brand/25 transition-all hover:scale-[1.01]"
                      >
                        <Route className="h-4 w-4" />
                        Preparar ruta
                      </button>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className="relative z-10 mt-5 flex flex-wrap gap-2">

                      key={category}
                      type="button"
                      onClick={() => setSelectedCategory(category as typeof selectedCategory)}

                        'rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-all',
                        selectedCategory === category
                          ? 'bg-brand text-white shadow-[0_14px_28px_rgba(255,99,33,0.24)]'

                            ? 'bg-white/8 text-white/76 hover:bg-white/12'
                            : 'bg-white text-slate-600 shadow-[0_10px_24px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)] hover:bg-slate-50'
                      )}
                    >
                      {category}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>

                <div className="relative z-10 mt-5 grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-3">
                  <div className={cn('rounded-[1.45rem] border px-4 py-4', isDarkMode ? 'border-white/10 bg-white/6' : 'border-white/80 bg-white/92 shadow-[0_16px_34px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)]')}>
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">

                    </div>
                    <p className="mt-2 text-[1.55rem] font-black leading-none">{String(filteredFallas.length).padStart(2, '0')}</p>
                    <p className="mt-2 text-[12px] font-bold leading-5 opacity-60">Comisiones listas para explorar desde el mapa.</p>

                      <p className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-brand">Foco actual</p>

                      {routeFocusFalla ? `${routeFocusFalla.neighborhood} | ${routeFocusFalla.section}` : 'La ficha y la ruta aparecerÃ¡n cuando selecciones una llama.'}

                  </div>
                </div>

                {routeFocusFalla && (

                        'inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-[1.15rem] px-4 py-3 text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-all',
                        isDarkMode ? 'bg-white text-slate-950 hover:bg-slate-100' : 'bg-slate-950 text-white hover:bg-slate-800'
                      )}
                    >
                      Abrir detalle
                    </button>
                    <button
                      type="button"
                      onClick={() => setActiveTab('Fallas')}
                      className={cn(
                        'inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-[1.15rem] px-4 py-3 text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-all',
                        isDarkMode ? 'bg-white/8 text-white/82 hover:bg-white/12' : 'bg-white text-slate-700 hover:bg-slate-50'

              <FallaMap
                isDarkMode={isDarkMode}

                    <h3 className="text-[2.15rem] font-black uppercase tracking-tighter">Monumentos top</h3>
                    <p className="text-sm font-bold opacity-55">SelecciÃ³n destacada para abrir detalle y moverte rÃ¡pido por los grandes focos del dashboard.</p>
                  </div>
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setActiveTab('Fallas')}
                    className={cn(
                      'inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-[1.15rem] px-4 py-3 text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-all',

                    )}

                    Ver catalogo
                    <ArrowRight className="h-4 w-4" />

                </div>
                <div className={cn('grid gap-8 md:grid-cols-2', !hasDockedNavigation && '2xl:grid-cols-4 xl:grid-cols-3')}>
                  {FALLAS_MOCK.slice(0, 4).map((falla) => (
                    <FallaCard key={falla.id} falla={falla} onClick={() => setShowDetail(falla)} />
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            {navigationFalla && (
              <div className="hidden min-w-0 xl:block">
                <div className="sticky top-8">
                  <NavigationErrorBoundary
                    isDarkMode={isDarkMode}
                    onReset={() => {
                      setNavigationFalla(null);
                      setActiveRouteFallaId(null);
                    }}
                  >
                    <NavigationMapDocked
                      falla={navigationFalla}
                      isDarkMode={isDarkMode}
                      mapStyleId={mapStyleId}
                      setMapStyleId={setMapStyleId}
                      activeRouteFallaId={activeRouteFallaId}
                      setActiveRouteFallaId={setActiveRouteFallaId}
                      userPosition={userPosition}
                      locationStatus={locationStatus}
                      requestLocation={requestLocation}
                      onClose={() => {
                        setNavigationFalla(null);
                        setActiveRouteFallaId(null);
                      }}
                    />
                  </NavigationErrorBoundary>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        );

      case 'Social':
        return (
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-8 xl:grid-cols-[320px_minmax(0,760px)] xl:items-start">

              <SectionHero
                isDarkMode={isDarkMode}

                  <DashboardMetric
                    isDarkMode={isDarkMode}

                    value={String(favorites.length).padStart(2, '0')}

                  />
                  <DashboardMetric
                    isDarkMode={isDarkMode}

                  />

              </SectionHero>
              <DashboardSurface isDarkMode={isDarkMode} className="space-y-4">
                <div>
                  <p className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-brand">Tendencias</p>
                  <h3 className="mt-2 text-[1.3rem] font-black leading-none tracking-tight">Lo que mas se esta moviendo ahora.</h3>
                </div>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                  {['#Fallas2026', '#Mascleta', '#Ofrenda', '#NitDelFoc'].map((tag) => (
                    <span
                      key={tag}
                      className={cn(
                        'rounded-full px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.14em]',

                      )}

                      {tag}
                    </span>
                  ))}
                </div>
                <div className="space-y-3">
                  {mostLikedPosts.map((post) => (
                    <div
                      key={post.id}
                      className={cn(

                        isDarkMode ? 'border-white/10 bg-white/6' : 'border-slate-100 bg-slate-50'

                    >
                      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
                        <p className="text-sm font-black">{post.user}</p>
                        <span className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-brand">{post.likes} likes</span>

                    Volver al mapa

                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setActiveTab('Agenda')}

                  >
                    Ver agenda
                  </button>

              </DashboardSurface>

            <div className="min-w-0">
              <SocialFeed isDarkMode={isDarkMode} posts={SOCIAL_POSTS} viewer={viewer} />

      case 'Agenda':
        return (

            <SectionHero
              isDarkMode={isDarkMode}

                          <span
                            className={cn(
                              'rounded-full px-3 py-1 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest',

                            )}

                            {event.type}

      case 'Fallas':

                      key={cat}

                        'rounded-2xl px-6 py-3 text-xs font-black uppercase tracking-widest transition-all',
                        selectedCategory === cat
                          ? 'bg-brand text-white shadow-xl shadow-brand/30'
                          : isDarkMode ? 'bg-white/5 text-white/60 hover:bg-white/10' : 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-500 hover:bg-gray-200'
                      )}
                    >
                      {cat}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
              {(searchQuery || selectedCategory !== 'Todas') && (
                <div className={cn('inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em]', isDarkMode ? 'bg-white/8 text-white/76' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-600')}>
                  {searchQuery ? `Busqueda: ${searchQuery}` : `Categoria: ${selectedCategory}`}
                </div>
              )}
            </DashboardSurface>

            {filteredFallas.length > 0 ? (
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-8 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3">
                {filteredFallas.map((falla) => (
                  <FallaCard key={falla.id} falla={falla} onClick={() => setShowDetail(falla)} />
                ))}
              </div>
            ) : (
              <DashboardSurface isDarkMode={isDarkMode} className="py-16 text-center">
                <p className="text-xl font-black uppercase tracking-widest opacity-45">No hay monumentos que coincidan con el filtro actual</p>
              </DashboardSurface>
            )}
          </div>
        );

      case 'TV':
        return <TVGuide isDarkMode={isDarkMode} channels={TV_CHANNELS} viewer={viewer} chatBot={TV_CHAT_BOT} />;

      case 'Perfil':
        return (
          <div className="space-y-8">
            <SectionHero
              isDarkMode={isDarkMode}
              eyebrow="Perfil"
              title={`Tu panel personal, ${viewer.name}.`}
              description="Configuracion, favoritos y contexto de uso en un mismo dashboard, con mas aire y mejor lectura que la version anterior."
              actions={
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => setIsProfileSettingsOpen(true)}
                  className={cn(
                    'inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-[1.15rem] px-4 py-3 text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-all',
                    isDarkMode ? 'bg-white text-slate-950 hover:bg-slate-100' : 'bg-slate-950 text-white hover:bg-slate-800'
                  )}
                >
                  <Settings2 className="h-4 w-4 text-brand" />
                  Configurar perfil
                </button>
              }
            >
              <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-3">
                <DashboardMetric
                  isDarkMode={isDarkMode}
                  icon={Heart}
                  label="Favoritos"
                  value={String(favorites.length).padStart(2, '0')}
                  helper="Monumentos guardados listos para volver al mapa."
                />
                <DashboardMetric
                  isDarkMode={isDarkMode}
                  icon={Eye}
                  label="Visitadas"
                  value="12"
                  helper="Historial visual estimado dentro del dashboard actual."
                />
                <DashboardMetric
                  isDarkMode={isDarkMode}
                  icon={MessageCircle}
                  label="Acceso"
                  value={viewer.accessType === 'guest' ? 'Invitado' : 'Registrado'}
                  helper={`Sesion activa en ${viewer.location}.`}
                />
              </div>
            </SectionHero>

            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-8 xl:grid-cols-[320px_minmax(0,1fr)]">
              <DashboardSurface isDarkMode={isDarkMode} className="space-y-5 xl:sticky xl:top-8">
                <div className="text-center">
                  <div className="relative inline-block">
                    <img src={viewer.avatar} alt={viewer.name} className="h-32 w-32 rounded-[3rem] border-4 border-brand object-cover shadow-2xl" />
                    <div className="absolute -bottom-2 -right-2 flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-brand text-white shadow-lg">
                      <Star className="h-5 w-5 fill-current" />
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <h2 className="mt-4 text-3xl font-black tracking-tight">{viewer.name}</h2>
                  <p className="mt-2 text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-brand">{viewer.handle}</p>
                  <p className="mt-3 text-sm font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] opacity-50">
                    {viewer.accessType === 'guest' ? 'Modo invitado' : 'Usuario registrado'} | {viewer.location}
                  </p>
                </div>

                <div className="grid gap-3">
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setActiveTab('Social')}
                    className={cn(
                      'inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-[1.2rem] px-4 py-3 text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-all',
                      isDarkMode ? 'bg-white/8 text-white hover:bg-white/12' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-700 hover:bg-slate-200'
                    )}
                  >
                    Abrir social
                  </button>
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setActiveTab('Fallas')}
                    className="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-[1.2rem] bg-brand px-4 py-3 text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] text-white shadow-xl shadow-brand/25 transition-all hover:scale-[1.01]"
                  >
                    Ver favoritas en catalogo
                  </button>
                </div>
              </DashboardSurface>

              <DashboardSurface isDarkMode={isDarkMode} className="space-y-4">
                <div className="flex flex-col gap-2 sm:flex-row sm:items-end sm:justify-between">
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-brand">Mis favoritas</p>
                    <h3 className="mt-2 text-[1.5rem] font-black leading-none tracking-tight">Tu seleccion guardada dentro del dashboard.</h3>
                  </div>
                  <span className={cn('inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full px-3 py-2 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em]', isDarkMode ? 'bg-white/8 text-white/76' : 'bg-slate-100 text-slate-600')}>
                    {favoriteFallas.length} monumentos
                  </span>
                </div>
                <div className="space-y-4">
                  {favoriteFallas.length > 0 ? (
                    favoriteFallas.map((falla) => (
                      <div
                        key={falla.id}
                        className={cn(
                          'flex items-center gap-4 rounded-3xl border p-4',
                          isDarkMode ? 'border-white/10 bg-white/5' : 'border-gray-100 bg-white shadow-md'
                        )}
                      >
                        <img src={falla.imageUrl} className="h-16 w-16 rounded-2xl object-cover" />
                        <div className="flex-1">
                          <p className="font-black">{falla.name}</p>
                          <p className="text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.12em] opacity-50">{falla.neighborhood}</p>
                        </div>
                        <button onClick={() => toggleFavorite(falla.id)} className="text-red-500">
                          <Heart className="h-5 w-5 fill-current" />
                        </button>
                      </div>
                    ))
                  ) : (
                    <div className="rounded-[2rem] border-2 border-dashed border-gray-300 py-10 text-center opacity-30">
                      <p className="text-sm font-black uppercase tracking-widest">Aun no tienes monumentos favoritos</p>
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              </DashboardSurface>
            </div>
          </div>
        );

      default:
        return null;
    }
  };

  return (
    <div
      className={cn(
        'min-h-screen pb-40 transition-colors duration-500 selection:bg-brand selection:text-white',
        isDarkMode ? 'bg-[#050505] text-white' : 'bg-[#F4F4F4] text-[#111111]'
      )}
    >
      <Header isDarkMode={isDarkMode} setIsDarkMode={setIsDarkMode} />

      <main
        className={cn(
          'mx-auto w-full space-y-12 pt-8',
          hasDockedNavigation
            ? 'max-w-none px-4 sm:px-5 xl:px-6 2xl:px-8'
            : isTvTab
              ? 'max-w-none px-3 sm:px-4 xl:px-6 2xl:px-8'
              : activeTab === 'Social'
                ? 'max-w-[1520px] px-4 sm:px-6 xl:px-10'
                : 'max-w-[1720px] px-4 sm:px-8 xl:px-10'
        )}
      >
        {showTopRail && (
          <div className="grid max-w-[1180px] grid-cols-1 items-stretch gap-6 xl:grid-cols-[minmax(320px,0.88fr)_minmax(0,1.26fr)]">
            <div className="min-w-0">
              <CountdownCard isDarkMode={isDarkMode} event={cridaEvent} />
            </div>
            <div className="min-w-0">
              <DateSelector
                isDarkMode={isDarkMode}
                selectedDate={selectedDate}
                setSelectedDate={setSelectedDate}
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        <AnimatePresence mode="wait">
          <motion.div
            key={activeTab}
            initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
          >
            {renderContent()}
          </motion.div>
        </AnimatePresence>
      </main>

      <FallaDetail
        falla={showDetail}
        onClose={() => setShowDetail(null)}
        onNavigateToFalla={handleNavigateToFalla}
        favorites={favorites}
        toggleFavorite={toggleFavorite}
      />

      <div className="xl:hidden">
        <NavigationErrorBoundary
          isDarkMode={isDarkMode}
          onReset={() => {
            setNavigationFalla(null);
            setActiveRouteFallaId(null);
          }}
        >
          <NavigationMapModal
            falla={navigationFalla}
            isDarkMode={isDarkMode}
            mapStyleId={mapStyleId}
            setMapStyleId={setMapStyleId}
            activeRouteFallaId={activeRouteFallaId}
            setActiveRouteFallaId={setActiveRouteFallaId}
            userPosition={userPosition}
            locationStatus={locationStatus}
            requestLocation={requestLocation}
            onClose={() => {
              setNavigationFalla(null);
              setActiveRouteFallaId(null);
            }}
          />
        </NavigationErrorBoundary>
      </div>

      <BottomNav
        isDarkMode={isDarkMode}
        activeTab={activeTab}
        setActiveTab={setActiveTab}
      />

      <AIAssistant
        isDarkMode={isDarkMode}
        activeTab={activeTab}
        selectedDate={selectedDate}
        selectedDateLabel={selectedDateLabel}
      />

      <ProfileSettingsModal
        isOpen={isProfileSettingsOpen}
        viewer={viewer}
        isDarkMode={isDarkMode}
        onClose={() => setIsProfileSettingsOpen(false)}
        onSave={handleSaveViewerSettings}
      />

      <div className="fixed inset-0 pointer-events-none z-[-1] overflow-hidden">
        <div
          className={cn(
            'absolute top-[-10%] right-[-10%] h-[50vw] w-[50vw] rounded-full blur-[120px] transition-opacity duration-1000',
            isDarkMode ? 'bg-brand/10 opacity-40' : 'bg-brand/5 opacity-60'
          )}
        />
        <div
          className={cn(
            'absolute bottom-[-10%] left-[-10%] h-[40vw] w-[40vw] rounded-full blur-[100px] transition-opacity duration-1000',
            isDarkMode ? 'bg-blue-900/10 opacity-30' : 'bg-blue-500/5 opacity-40'
          )}
        />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: src\components\AIAssistant.tsx

import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState } from 'react';
import { AnimatePresence, motion } from 'motion/react';
import { Bot, LoaderCircle, SendHorizontal, Sparkles, X } from 'lucide-react';
import { cn } from '../utils/cn';

type ChatRole = 'user' | 'assistant';

type ChatMessage = {
  id: string;
  role: ChatRole;
  content: string;
};

interface AIAssistantProps {
  isDarkMode: boolean;
  activeTab: string;
  selectedDate: string;
  selectedDateLabel: string;
}

const STARTER_SUGGESTIONS = [
  'RecomiÃ©ndame un plan fallero para esta noche en Valencia.',
  'Dime una ruta corta para ver fallas sin andar demasiado.',
  'QuÃ© actos priorizarÃ­as hoy si solo tengo 3 horas.',
];

function createMessage(role: ChatRole, content: string): ChatMessage {
  return {
    id: crypto.randomUUID(),
    role,
    content,
  };
}

export function AIAssistant({ isDarkMode, activeTab, selectedDate, selectedDateLabel }: AIAssistantProps) {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
  const [inputValue, setInputValue] = useState('');
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<ChatMessage[]>([
    createMessage(
      'assistant',
      'Soy tu asistente fallero. Puedo proponerte rutas, actos y planes rÃ¡pidos segÃºn la fecha y la pestaÃ±a en la que estÃ¡s.'
    ),
  ]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [modelUsed, setModelUsed] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const scrollAreaRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isOpen || !scrollAreaRef.current) {
      return;
    }

    scrollAreaRef.current.scrollTop = scrollAreaRef.current.scrollHeight;
  }, [isOpen, messages, isLoading]);

  const canSend = inputValue.trim().length > 0 && !isLoading;

  const assistantContext = useMemo(
    () => ({
      activeTab,
      selectedDate,
      selectedDateLabel,
    }),
    [activeTab, selectedDate, selectedDateLabel]
  );

  const sendMessage = async (content: string) => {
    const trimmed = content.trim();

    if (!trimmed || isLoading) {
      return;
    }

    const userMessage = createMessage('user', trimmed);
    const outgoingMessages = [...messages, userMessage];

    setMessages(outgoingMessages);
    setInputValue('');
    setError(null);
    setIsLoading(true);

    try {
      const response = await fetch('/api/assistant', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          messages: outgoingMessages.map(({ role, content: messageContent }) => ({
            role,
            content: messageContent,
          })),
          context: assistantContext,
        }),
      });

      const payload = await response.json().catch(() => ({}));

      if (!response.ok) {
        throw new Error(payload.message || 'No se pudo obtener respuesta del asistente.');
      }

      setModelUsed(payload.model || null);
      setMessages((currentMessages) => [
        ...currentMessages,
        createMessage('assistant', payload.content || 'No he podido generar una respuesta Ãºtil.'),
      ]);
    } catch (requestError) {
      const fallbackMessage =
        requestError instanceof Error ? requestError.message : 'Error inesperado al consultar el asistente.';

      setError(fallbackMessage);
    } finally {
      setIsLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <>
      <button
        type="button"
        onClick={() => setIsOpen(true)}
        className={cn(
          'fixed right-5 bottom-[8.5rem] z-[5200] inline-flex items-center gap-3 rounded-full px-4 py-3 shadow-[0_20px_40px_rgba(255,99,33,0.24)] transition-all',
          isDarkMode ? 'bg-[#121212] text-white border border-white/10' : 'bg-white text-slate-950 border border-orange-100'
        )}
      >
        <span className="flex h-11 w-11 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-brand text-white shadow-[0_12px_24px_rgba(255,99,33,0.28)]">
          <Bot className="w-5 h-5" />
        </span>
        <span className="hidden sm:block text-left">
          <span className="block text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-brand">Asistente IA</span>
          <span className={cn('block text-xs font-bold', isDarkMode ? 'text-white/72' : 'text-slate-500')}>
            Planes y recomendaciones
          </span>
        </span>
      </button>

      <AnimatePresence>
        {isOpen && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
            className="fixed inset-0 z-[6000] bg-black/30 backdrop-blur-[8px] p-4 sm:p-6"
            onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}
          >
            <motion.div
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 32, scale: 0.96 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0, scale: 1 }}
              exit={{ opacity: 0, y: 24, scale: 0.98 }}
              transition={{ duration: 0.22 }}
              onClick={(event) => event.stopPropagation()}
              className={cn(
                'mx-auto mt-[8vh] flex w-full max-w-[460px] flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-[2rem] border shadow-[0_32px_80px_rgba(15,23,42,0.26)]',
                isDarkMode ? 'bg-[#0d0d0d] border-white/10 text-white' : 'bg-[#fffaf6] border-orange-100 text-slate-950'
              )}
            >
              <div className={cn(
                'flex items-start justify-between gap-4 border-b px-5 py-5',
                isDarkMode ? 'border-white/10 bg-white/[0.03]' : 'border-orange-100 bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,#fff8f3_0%,#fff4ec_100%)]'
              )}>
                <div className="min-w-0">
                  <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full bg-brand/10 px-3 py-1 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-brand">
                    <Sparkles className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                    Asistente Fallero
                  </div>
                  <h3 className="mt-3 text-xl font-black tracking-tight">Pregunta y te propongo un plan</h3>
                  <p className={cn('mt-1 text-sm', isDarkMode ? 'text-white/58' : 'text-slate-500')}>
                    Contexto: {activeTab} Â· {selectedDateLabel}
                  </p>
                </div>

                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)}
                  className={cn(
                    'flex h-11 w-11 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl transition-colors',
                    isDarkMode ? 'bg-white/5 text-white/70 hover:bg-white/10' : 'bg-white text-slate-400 hover:bg-orange-50'
                  )}
                >
                  <X className="w-5 h-5" />
                </button>
              </div>

              <div ref={scrollAreaRef} className="max-h-[52vh] min-h-[360px] space-y-4 overflow-y-auto px-5 py-5 custom-scrollbar">
                {messages.map((message) => (
                  <div
                    key={message.id}
                    className={cn(
                      'max-w-[88%] rounded-[1.4rem] px-4 py-3 text-sm leading-6 shadow-sm',
                      message.role === 'assistant'
                        ? isDarkMode
                          ? 'bg-white/5 text-white/88'
                          : 'bg-white text-slate-700 border border-orange-50'
                        : 'ml-auto bg-brand text-white'
                    )}
                  >
                    {message.content}
                  </div>
                ))}

                {isLoading && (
                  <div className={cn(
                    'inline-flex items-center gap-3 rounded-[1.4rem] px-4 py-3 text-sm',
                    isDarkMode ? 'bg-white/5 text-white/70' : 'bg-white text-slate-500 border border-orange-50'
                  )}>
                    <LoaderCircle className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin" />
                    Pensando una respuesta...
                  </div>
                )}

                {error && (
                  <div className="rounded-[1.2rem] border border-red-200 bg-red-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-red-700">
                    {error}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>

              <div className="border-t px-5 py-4">
                <div className="mb-3 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                  {STARTER_SUGGESTIONS.map((suggestion) => (
                    <button
                      key={suggestion}
                      type="button"
                      onClick={() => void sendMessage(suggestion)}
                      disabled={isLoading}
                      className={cn(
                        'rounded-full px-3 py-2 text-[11px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.12em] transition-colors',
                        isDarkMode
                          ? 'bg-white/6 text-white/72 hover:bg-white/10 disabled:opacity-50'
                          : 'bg-orange-50 text-brand hover:bg-orange-100 disabled:opacity-50'
                      )}
                    >
                      {suggestion}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>

                <div className={cn(
                  'flex items-end gap-3 rounded-[1.6rem] border p-3',
                  isDarkMode ? 'border-white/10 bg-white/[0.03]' : 'border-orange-100 bg-white'
                )}>
                  <textarea
                    value={inputValue}
                    onChange={(event) => setInputValue(event.target.value)}
                    onKeyDown={(event) => {
                      if (event.key === 'Enter' && !event.shiftKey) {
                        event.preventDefault();
                        void sendMessage(inputValue);
                      }
                    }}
                    placeholder="Escribe tu pregunta fallera..."
                    rows={1}
                    className={cn(
                      'max-h-32 min-h-[52px] flex-1 resize-none bg-transparent px-1 py-2 text-sm outline-none',
                      isDarkMode ? 'text-white placeholder:text-white/35' : 'text-slate-700 placeholder:text-slate-400'
                    )}
                  />
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => void sendMessage(inputValue)}
                    disabled={!canSend}
                    className="flex h-12 w-12 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-brand text-white shadow-[0_12px_24px_rgba(255,99,33,0.24)] disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50"
                  >
                    <SendHorizontal className="w-5 h-5" />
                  </button>
                </div>

                <div className={cn(
                  'mt-3 flex items-center justify-between text-[11px]',
                  isDarkMode ? 'text-white/40' : 'text-slate-400'
                )}>
                  <span>Respuesta breve y Ãºtil.</span>
                  <span>{modelUsed ? `Modelo: ${modelUsed}` : 'OpenRouter'}</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </motion.div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>
    </>
  );
}

import React from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'motion/react';
import { Map as MapIcon, Calendar, Flame, MessageCircle, Tv, User } from 'lucide-react';
import { cn } from '../utils/cn';

interface BottomNavProps {
  isDarkMode: boolean;
  activeTab: string;
  setActiveTab: (tab: string) => void;
}

export function BottomNav({ isDarkMode, activeTab, setActiveTab }: BottomNavProps) {
  const tabs = [
    { icon: MapIcon, label: 'Mapa' },
    { icon: Calendar, label: 'Agenda' },
    { icon: MessageCircle, label: 'Social' },
    { icon: Tv, label: 'TV' },
    { icon: Flame, label: 'Fallas' },
    { icon: User, label: 'Perfil' }
  ];

  return (
    <nav className="fixed bottom-6 left-1/2 z-[5000] w-[94%] max-w-3xl -translate-x-1/2 sm:bottom-8">
      <div className={cn(
        "backdrop-blur-3xl border shadow-[0_40px_80px_rgba(0,0,0,0.4)] rounded-[2.5rem] p-1.5 sm:p-2 flex items-center justify-between transition-all duration-500",
        isDarkMode ? "bg-black/45 border-white/10" : "bg-white/72 border-black/5"
      )}>
        {tabs.map((item) => {
          const isActive = activeTab === item.label;
          return (
            <button
              key={item.label}
              onClick={() => setActiveTab(item.label)}
              className={cn(
                "relative min-w-0 flex-1 flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1 py-3.5 sm:gap-1.5 sm:py-4 rounded-[1.8rem] sm:rounded-[2rem] transition-all duration-500 group outline-none",
                isActive
                  ? "text-white"
                  : isDarkMode
                    ? "text-white/80 hover:text-white"
                    : "text-slate-700 hover:text-slate-950"
              )}
            >
              <AnimatePresence>
                {isActive && (
                  <motion.div 
                    layoutId="nav-pill-premium"
                    className="absolute inset-0 bg-brand z-0 shadow-[0_10px_30px_rgba(255,100,0,0.4)]"
                    style={{ borderRadius: '1.8rem' }}
                    transition={{ type: "spring", bounce: 0.2, duration: 0.6 }}
                  />
                )}
              </AnimatePresence>
              
              <div
                className={cn(
                  "relative z-10 rounded-2xl p-2 sm:p-2.5 transition-all duration-500",
                  isActive
                    ? "bg-transparent"
                    : isDarkMode
                      ? "bg-white/8 border border-white/10 shadow-[0_8px_24px_rgba(0,0,0,0.28)]"
                      : "bg-slate-100 border border-slate-200 shadow-[0_8px_24px_rgba(15,23,42,0.08)]"
                )}
              >
                <item.icon className={cn(
                  "h-5 w-5 transition-all duration-500 sm:h-5.5 sm:w-5.5",
                  isActive ? "scale-110" : "group-hover:scale-110 group-active:scale-90"
                )} />
                {isActive && (
                  <motion.div 
                    layoutId="active-dot"
                    className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 w-2 h-2 bg-white rounded-full border-2 border-brand"
                  />
                )}
              </div>

              <span className={cn(
                "relative z-10 truncate text-[8px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.16em] transition-all duration-500 sm:text-[9px] sm:tracking-[0.2em]",
                isActive
                  ? "opacity-100 translate-y-0"

              )}
            </button>
          );

  );
}

FILE: src\components\CountdownCard.tsx

import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { MapPin, Play } from 'lucide-react';
import { type Event } from '../data';
import { cn } from '../utils/cn';
import { formatShortDateTime, getCountdownParts, getNextRecurringEventDate } from '../utils/date';

interface CountdownCardProps {
  isDarkMode: boolean;
  event: Event | null;
}

export function CountdownCard({ isDarkMode, event }: CountdownCardProps) {
  const [now, setNow] = useState(() => new Date());

  useEffect(() => {
    const timer = window.setInterval(() => {
      setNow(new Date());
    }, 1000);

    return () => window.clearInterval(timer);
  }, []);

  const nextOccurrence = useMemo(() => {
    if (!event) {
      return null;
    }

    return getNextRecurringEventDate(event.date, event.time, now);
  }, [event, now]);

  const countdown = useMemo(() => {
    if (!nextOccurrence) {
      return { days: 0, hours: 0, minutes: 0, seconds: 0 };
    }

    return getCountdownParts(nextOccurrence, now);
  }, [nextOccurrence, now]);

  const countdownUnits = [
    { value: countdown.days, label: 'D' },
    { value: countdown.hours, label: 'H' },
    { value: countdown.minutes, label: 'M' },
    { value: countdown.seconds, label: 'S' },
  ];

  return (
    <section className="relative group h-full">
      <div
        className={cn(
          'h-full rounded-[2.5rem] p-7 flex flex-col justify-between overflow-hidden relative transition-all duration-500',
          isDarkMode ? 'bg-[#111] border border-white/10' : 'bg-white border border-gray-200 shadow-xl'
        )}
      >
        <div className="relative z-10">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-5 gap-4">
            <span className="px-2.5 py-1 bg-brand/10 text-brand rounded-full text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest">
              Cuenta atrÃ¡s
            </span>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-[11px] font-bold opacity-50 min-w-0">
              <MapPin className="w-3 h-3 shrink-0" />
              <span className="truncate">{event?.location ?? 'Sin ubicaciÃ³n'}</span>
            </div>
          </div>

          <h3 className="text-[2rem] font-black tracking-tighter leading-none mb-1.5">
            {event?.title ?? 'PrÃ³ximo acto'}
          </h3>
          <p className="text-[13px] opacity-50 font-medium">
            {nextOccurrence ? formatShortDateTime(nextOccurrence) : 'Fecha pendiente'}
          </p>
        </div>

        <div className="mt-6 flex items-end justify-between gap-4 relative z-10">
          <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 flex-1 min-w-0">
            {countdownUnits.map((unit) => (
              <div key={unit.label} className="flex flex-col items-center min-w-0">
                <div
                  className={cn(
                    'w-full h-[4.5rem] rounded-[1.25rem] flex items-center justify-center text-[1.45rem] font-black mb-1.5 border-b-[3px]',
                    isDarkMode ? 'bg-white/5 border-brand' : 'bg-gray-50 border-brand shadow-inner'
                  )}
                >
                  {String(unit.value).padStart(unit.label === 'D' ? 3 : 2, '0')}
                </div>
                <span className="text-[9px] font-black opacity-40">{unit.label}</span>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>

          <button className="w-14 h-14 shrink-0 bg-brand rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-white shadow-2xl shadow-brand/40 hover:scale-110 transition-transform">
            <Play className="w-5 h-5 fill-current" />
          </button>
        </div>

        <div
          className="absolute inset-0 opacity-[0.03] pointer-events-none"
          style={{ backgroundImage: 'radial-gradient(circle, currentColor 1px, transparent 1px)', backgroundSize: '20px 20px' }}
        />
      </div>
    </section>
  );
}

FILE: src\components\DateSelector.tsx
================================================================================
import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { createPortal } from 'react-dom';
import { ChevronLeft, ChevronRight, Flame, Maximize2, Minimize2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { cn } from '../utils/cn';
import {
  addMonths,
  formatLongDate,
  formatMonthYear,
  formatShortMonth,
  formatShortWeekday,
  fromIsoDate,
  getCompactDateStrip,
  getMonthGrid,
  getWeekdayLabels,
  isSameDay,
  isSameMonth,
  startOfMonth,
  toIsoDate,
} from '../utils/date';

interface DateSelectorProps {
  isDarkMode: boolean;
  selectedDate: string;
  setSelectedDate: (date: string) => void;
}

const FALLAS_MONTH_INDEX = 2;
const FALLAS_WEEK_START_DAY = 15;
const FALLAS_WEEK_END_DAY = 19;

export function DateSelector({ isDarkMode, selectedDate, setSelectedDate }: DateSelectorProps) {
  const [isExpanded, setIsExpanded] = useState(false);
  const selectedDateValue = useMemo(() => fromIsoDate(selectedDate), [selectedDate]);
  const today = useMemo(() => fromIsoDate(toIsoDate(new Date())), []);
  const [visibleMonth, setVisibleMonth] = useState(() => startOfMonth(selectedDateValue));

  useEffect(() => {
    setVisibleMonth((currentMonth) => (
      isSameMonth(currentMonth, selectedDateValue) ? currentMonth : startOfMonth(selectedDateValue)
    ));
  }, [selectedDateValue]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isExpanded) {
      return undefined;
    }

    const originalOverflow = document.body.style.overflow;

    const handleKeyDown = (event: KeyboardEvent) => {
      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        setIsExpanded(false);
      }
    };

    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    window.addEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);

    return () => {
      document.body.style.overflow = originalOverflow;
      window.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKeyDown);
    };
  }, [isExpanded]);

  const compactDates = useMemo(() => getCompactDateStrip(selectedDateValue), [selectedDateValue]);
  const monthGrid = useMemo(() => getMonthGrid(visibleMonth), [visibleMonth]);
  const monthWeeks = useMemo(
    () => Array.from({ length: monthGrid.length / 7 }, (_, index) => monthGrid.slice(index * 7, index * 7 + 7)),
    [monthGrid]
  );
  const weekdayLabels = useMemo(() => getWeekdayLabels(), []);
  const isFallasMonth = visibleMonth.getMonth() === FALLAS_MONTH_INDEX;

  const isFallasDate = (date: Date) => (
    date.getMonth() === FALLAS_MONTH_INDEX
    && date.getDate() >= FALLAS_WEEK_START_DAY
    && date.getDate() <= FALLAS_WEEK_END_DAY
  );

  const fallasWeekIndex = useMemo(
    () => monthWeeks.findIndex((week) => week.some((date) => date && isFallasDate(date))),
    [monthWeeks]
  );

  const getDayButtonClassName = (date: Date) => {
    const selected = isSameDay(date, selectedDateValue);
    const isToday = isSameDay(date, today);

    if (selected) {
      return 'bg-brand border-brand text-white shadow-2xl shadow-brand/40 scale-[1.03]';
    }

    if (isToday) {
      return isDarkMode
        ? 'bg-brand/10 border-brand/40 text-white'
        : 'bg-brand/10 border-brand/50 text-brand';
    }

    if (isFallasDate(date)) {
      return isDarkMode
        ? 'bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(255,138,76,0.22),rgba(255,90,40,0.16))] border-orange-300/35 text-white shadow-[0_16px_28px_rgba(255,98,53,0.16)]'
        : 'bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,#fff7f2_0%,#fff3ec_100%)] border-[#ffb287] text-[#a8431f] shadow-[0_16px_28px_rgba(255,98,53,0.12)]';
    }

    if (isFallasMonth) {
      return isDarkMode
        ? 'bg-white/5 border-white/5 text-white/54 hover:bg-white/10'
        : 'bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.94),rgba(248,248,249,0.96))] border-white/70 text-slate-400 shadow-[0_8px_18px_rgba(148,163,184,0.08)] hover:bg-white';
    }

    return isDarkMode
      ? 'bg-white/5 border-transparent text-white/40 hover:bg-white/10'
      : 'bg-gray-50 border-transparent text-gray-400 hover:bg-gray-100';
  };

  const expandedCalendar =
    isExpanded && typeof document !== 'undefined'
      ? createPortal(
          <div
            className="fixed inset-0 z-[7000] flex items-center justify-center bg-[rgba(15,23,42,0.28)] backdrop-blur-[10px] p-4 sm:p-6"
            onClick={() => setIsExpanded(false)}
          >
            <div
              className={cn(
                'relative overflow-hidden w-full max-w-[860px] rounded-[2.4rem] p-6 sm:p-8 border shadow-[0_32px_100px_rgba(15,23,42,0.22)]',
                isDarkMode ? 'bg-[#111]/95 border-white/10 text-white' : 'bg-white/96 border-gray-200 text-[#111111]',
                isFallasMonth && (
                  isDarkMode
                    ? 'bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_right,rgba(255,126,67,0.16),transparent_24%),linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(17,17,17,0.98),rgba(17,17,17,0.94))]'
                    : 'bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,#fffaf6_0%,#fff6ef_100%)] border-[#f2dfd2]'
                )
              )}
              onClick={(event) => event.stopPropagation()}
            >
              {isFallasMonth && !isDarkMode && (
                <>
                  <div className="pointer-events-none absolute -right-10 -top-10 h-44 w-44 rounded-full bg-[radial-gradient(circle,rgba(255,176,120,0.34)_0%,rgba(255,176,120,0)_72%)]" />
                  <div className="pointer-events-none absolute right-8 top-0 h-36 w-36 rounded-full bg-[radial-gradient(circle,rgba(255,136,72,0.16)_0%,rgba(255,136,72,0)_76%)]" />
                  <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 opacity-[0.04]" style={{ backgroundImage: 'radial-gradient(circle, currentColor 1px, transparent 1px)', backgroundSize: '18px 18px' }} />
                </>
              )}

              <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-4 mb-6">
                <div>
                  <h3 className="text-[1.4rem] sm:text-[1.55rem] font-black tracking-tight">Calendario Fallero</h3>
                  <p className="mt-1 text-[11px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] opacity-45">
                    {formatMonthYear(visibleMonth)}
                  </p>
                  {isFallasMonth && (
                    <div className={cn(
                      'mt-3 inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full px-3 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em]',
                      isDarkMode ? 'bg-brand/10 text-brand' : 'bg-[#fff0e5] text-brand shadow-[0_8px_18px_rgba(255,99,33,0.08)]'
                    )}>
                      <Flame className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                      Mes Fallero
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>

                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setVisibleMonth((currentMonth) => addMonths(currentMonth, -1))}
                    className={cn(
                      'p-2 rounded-[1rem] text-brand',
                      isFallasMonth && !isDarkMode ? 'bg-[#fff0e5] shadow-[0_10px_20px_rgba(255,99,33,0.08)]' : 'bg-brand/10'
                    )}
                    aria-label="Mes anterior"
                  >
                    <ChevronLeft className="w-4 h-4" />
                  </button>
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setVisibleMonth((currentMonth) => addMonths(currentMonth, 1))}
                    className={cn(
                      'p-2 rounded-[1rem] text-brand',
                      isFallasMonth && !isDarkMode ? 'bg-[#fff0e5] shadow-[0_10px_20px_rgba(255,99,33,0.08)]' : 'bg-brand/10'
                    )}
                    aria-label="Mes siguiente"
                  >
                    <ChevronRight className="w-4 h-4" />
                  </button>
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setIsExpanded(false)}
                    className={cn(
                      'inline-flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-[1rem] text-brand text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em]',
                      isFallasMonth && !isDarkMode ? 'bg-[#ffe8da] shadow-[0_10px_20px_rgba(255,99,33,0.08)]' : 'bg-brand/10'
                    )}
                  >
                    <Minimize2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
                    Cerrar
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className={cn('space-y-3', isFallasMonth && 'relative z-10')}>
                <div className="grid grid-cols-7 gap-2">
                  {weekdayLabels.map((label) => (
                    <div
                      key={label}
                      className={cn(
                        'text-center text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em] opacity-40 py-1',
                        isFallasMonth && !isDarkMode && 'text-[#9d938f]'
                      )}
                    >
                      {label}
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>

                <div className="space-y-2 sm:space-y-3">
                  {monthWeeks.map((week, weekIndex) => {
                    const isFallasWeek = isFallasMonth && weekIndex === fallasWeekIndex;

                    return (
                      <div
                        key={`week-${weekIndex}`}
                        className={cn(
                          'grid grid-cols-7 gap-2 sm:gap-3 rounded-[1.5rem] transition-all',
                          isFallasWeek && (
                            isDarkMode
                              ? 'bg-[linear-gradient(90deg,rgba(255,117,79,0.12),rgba(255,170,122,0.06))] p-2 border border-orange-300/15'
                              : 'bg-[linear-gradient(90deg,#fff0e5_0%,#fff7f2_100%)] p-2 border border-[#ffc59f] shadow-[0_12px_24px_rgba(255,99,33,0.08)]'
                          )
                        )}
                      >
                        {week.map((date, index) => {
                          if (!date) {
                            return <div key={`empty-${weekIndex}-${index}`} className="aspect-square rounded-[1.2rem]" aria-hidden="true" />;
                          }

                          return (
                            <button
                              key={toIsoDate(date)}
                              type="button"
                              onClick={() => {
                                setSelectedDate(toIsoDate(date));
                                setIsExpanded(false);
                              }}
                              className={cn(
                                'aspect-square rounded-[1.2rem] border transition-all flex flex-col items-center justify-center',
                                getDayButtonClassName(date)
                              )}
                            >
                              <span className="text-[1rem] sm:text-[1.15rem] font-black leading-none">{date.getDate()}</span>
                              <span className="mt-1 text-[8px] sm:text-[9px] font-black opacity-55">{formatShortMonth(date)}</span>
                            </button>
                          );
                        })}
                      </div>
                    );
                  })}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>,
          document.body
        )
      : null;

  return (
    <>
      <section className="h-full">
        <div
          className={cn(
            'relative overflow-hidden h-full rounded-[2.5rem] p-7 transition-all duration-500',
            isDarkMode ? 'bg-white/5' : 'bg-white shadow-xl border border-gray-100',
            selectedDateValue.getMonth() === FALLAS_MONTH_INDEX && (
              isDarkMode
                ? 'bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_right,rgba(255,126,67,0.12),transparent_28%),linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.05),rgba(255,255,255,0.04))] border-orange-300/15'
                : 'bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,#fffaf6_0%,#fff6ef_100%)] border-[#f2dfd2]'
            )
          )}
        >
          {selectedDateValue.getMonth() === FALLAS_MONTH_INDEX && !isDarkMode && (
            <>
              <div className="pointer-events-none absolute -right-6 -top-8 h-28 w-28 rounded-full bg-[radial-gradient(circle,rgba(255,176,120,0.26)_0%,rgba(255,176,120,0)_74%)]" />
              <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 opacity-[0.04]" style={{ backgroundImage: 'radial-gradient(circle, currentColor 1px, transparent 1px)', backgroundSize: '18px 18px' }} />
            </>
          )}

          <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3 mb-6">
            <div>
              <h3 className="text-[1.1rem] font-black tracking-tight">Calendario Fallero</h3>
              <p className="mt-1 text-[11px] font-bold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] opacity-45">
                {formatLongDate(selectedDateValue)}
              </p>
              {selectedDateValue.getMonth() === FALLAS_MONTH_INDEX && (
                <div className={cn(
                  'mt-3 inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full px-3 py-1 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-brand',
                  isDarkMode ? 'bg-brand/10' : 'bg-[#fff0e5] shadow-[0_8px_18px_rgba(255,99,33,0.08)]'
                )}>
                  <Flame className="w-3 h-3" />
                  Semana Fallera
                </div>
              )}
            </div>

            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setIsExpanded(true)}
              className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-[0.95rem] bg-brand/10 text-brand text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-[0.18em]"
            >
              <Maximize2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
              Mes
            </button>
          </div>

          <div className="grid grid-cols-5 gap-3">
            {compactDates.map((date) => (
              <button
                key={toIsoDate(date)}
                type="button"
                onClick={() => setSelectedDate(toIsoDate(date))}
                className={cn(
                  'aspect-[5/7] rounded-[1.6rem] flex flex-col items-center justify-center transition-all border',
                  getDayButtonClassName(date)
                )}
              >
                <span className="text-[9px] font-black opacity-60 mb-0.5">{formatShortWeekday(date)}</span>
                <span className="text-[1.85rem] font-black leading-none">{date.getDate()}</span>
                <span className="text-[9px] font-black opacity-60 mt-0.5">{formatShortMonth(date)}</span>
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </section>
      {expandedCalendar}
    </>
  );
}
